info:Business Room (Double bed)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Business travelers
info:7 Reviews
rating:3
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:Because the order on Ctrip did not include breakfast, the hotel also refused to provide free meal coupons, which may be a rare principle that most hotels adhere to. Under such excellent quality, I thought that a hotel that costs three or four hundred yuan a night should at least provide normal check-in conditions without asking for surprises. As a result, the water used for washing, including the sink and bathtub, was room temperature water, and no matter how high it was turned, it felt like boiled water. Can't understand how difficult it is to boil water? Of course, after feedback, the hotel was very active in trying to solve it, but it was really troublesome at more than 10 o'clock in the evening. And the faucet was still dripping at night. So the check-in experience was very poor.
